#############
# Resource buildings
#############

building_nanite_fabricator_1 = {
	base_buildtime = @b3_time

	category = manufacturing

	destroy_trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_modifier = resort_colony
			has_modifier = slave_colony
			AND = {
				exists = owner
				buildings_no_motes = yes
				buildings_no_crystals = yes
				buildings_no_exotic_gases = yes
			}
		}
	}

	allow = {
		has_upgraded_capital = yes
	}

	triggered_planet_modifier = {
		potential = {
			exists = owner
			owner = { is_gestalt = no }
		}
		modifier = {
			job_nanoroboticist_add = 1
		}
	}

	triggered_planet_modifier = {
		potential = {
			exists = owner
			owner = { is_gestalt = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			job_nanoroboticist_drone_add = 1
		}
	}

	resources = {
		category = planet_buildings
		cost = {
			alloys = 1000
		}
		upkeep = {
			rare_crystals = 2
			volatile_motes = 2
			exotic_gases = 2
			energy = 5
		}
	}

	upgrades = {
		building_nanite_fabricator_2
	}

	prerequisites = {
		"tech_micromechanic_constructs"
	}

	ai_resource_production = {
		nanites = 2
		trigger = {
			always = yes
		}
	}
}

building_nanite_fabricator_2 = {
	base_buildtime = @b3_time
	can_build = no
	category = manufacturing

	destroy_trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_modifier = resort_colony
			has_modifier = slave_colony
			AND = {
				exists = owner
				buildings_no_motes = yes
				buildings_no_crystals = yes
				buildings_no_exotic_gases = yes
			}
		}
	}

	allow = {
		has_upgraded_capital = yes
	}

	triggered_planet_modifier = {
		potential = {
			exists = owner
			owner = { is_gestalt = no }
		}
		modifier = {
			job_nanoroboticist_add = 3
		}
	}

	triggered_planet_modifier = {
		potential = {
			exists = owner
			owner = { is_gestalt = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			job_nanoroboticist_drone_add = 3
		}
	}

	resources = {
		category = planet_buildings
		cost = {
			alloys = 1000
		}
		upkeep = {
			rare_crystals = 3
			volatile_motes = 3
			exotic_gases = 3
			energy = 10
		}
	}

	upgrades = {
		building_nanite_fabricator_3
	}

	prerequisites = {
		"tech_nanoscale_automatons"
	}

	ai_resource_production = {
		nanites = 6
		trigger = {
			always = yes
		}
	}
}

building_nanite_fabricator_3 = {
	base_buildtime = @b3_time

	category = manufacturing
	can_build = no
	destroy_trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_modifier = resort_colony
			has_modifier = slave_colony
			AND = {
				exists = owner
				buildings_no_motes = yes
				buildings_no_crystals = yes
				buildings_no_exotic_gases = yes
			}
		}
	}

	allow = {
		has_upgraded_capital = yes
	}

	triggered_planet_modifier = {
		potential = {
			exists = owner
			owner = { is_gestalt = no }
		}
		modifier = {
			job_nanoroboticist_add = 5
		}
	}

	triggered_planet_modifier = {
		potential = {
			exists = owner
			owner = { is_gestalt = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			job_nanoroboticist_drone_add = 5
		}
	}

	resources = {
		category = planet_buildings
		cost = {
			alloys = 1000
		}
		upkeep = {
			rare_crystals = 5
			volatile_motes = 5
			exotic_gases = 5
			energy = 15
		}
	}

	prerequisites = {
		"tech_femtoscale_robotics"
	}

	ai_resource_production = {
		nanites = 10
		trigger = {
			always = yes
		}
	}
}

building_universal_constructor_1 = {
	base_buildtime = @b1_time
	base_cap_amount = 1
	category = manufacturing

	potential = {
		NOT = { has_modifier = resort_colony }
		NOT = { has_modifier = slave_colony }
		OR = {
			building_relaxed_basic_income_check = yes
		}
	}

	allow = {
		has_upgraded_capital = yes
	}

	destroy_trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_modifier = resort_colony
			has_modifier = slave_colony
		}
	}

	resources = {
		category = planet_buildings

		# Normal Planets Tier 1
        produces = { 
			trigger = { 
				planet = {
					num_districts = { 
						type = district_industrial value > 0
					}
				} 
			} 
			alloys = 2
			consumer_goods = 2
			nanites = -1
		}
        produces = { 
			trigger = { 
				owner = {
					has_technology = tech_atto_optimizations
				}
				planet = {
					num_districts = { 
						type = district_industrial value > 0
					}
				} 
			} 
			alloys = 2
			consumer_goods = 2
			nanites = -1
		}

				}

			consumer_goods = 2
			nanites = -1
		}

			trigger = { 
				owner = {
					has_technology = tech_atto_optimizations
				}
